# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# VML BALNEOLOGICAL (BATH) SECTION — COMPLETE ANALYSIS
# Folios f75r through f84v — The Purification Infrastructure
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# SECTION INTRODUCTION — WHY THE BATH SECTION MATTERS

## Position in the Manuscript

The Bath section occupies 20 folios (f75r–f84v) and sits between the Astrological section (the CLOCK) and the Pharmaceutical section (the RECIPES). This is not an accident of binding — it is the LOGICAL INTERMEDIARY:

- **Herbal Section (f1r–f57r):** RAW MATERIALS — what to gather, how to process single plants
- **Astrological Section (f58r–f73v):** TIMING — when to gather, when to process
- **Bath Section (f75r–f84v):** PURIFICATION — how to refine raw materials into usable fractions
- **Pharmaceutical Section (f87r–f116v):** RECIPES — how to combine purified fractions into medicines

The Bath section is the FACTORY FLOOR. It transforms the herbal section's raw plant materials into the pharmaceutical section's refined ingredients. Without it, you have herbs and recipes but no way to get from one to the other.

## The Dual Reading

Every bath page sustains TWO simultaneous valid interpretations:

1. **HYDROTHERAPY:** Pools are baths, tubes carry water, nymphs are patients following a bathing sequence. Medieval bath houses were genuine medical facilities — hydrotherapy was prescribed for everything from fever to melancholy.

2. **DISTILLATION:** Pools are vessels (retorts, alembics, receivers), tubes are condensers and channels, nymphs are process-state indicators showing what condition the material is in at each node. The circulation of bath water mirrors the circulation of distillate.

A sophisticated 15th-century practitioner read BOTH meanings simultaneously. The body IS an alembic; the bath DOES work like distillation. Microcosm = macrocosm. This dual reading is not ambiguity — it is deliberate multivalence, consistent with the manuscript's layered encoding strategy throughout.

## The Spatial Grammar — Rules Unique to This Section

The bath section introduces THREE spatial grammar rules that do not apply to the herbal or astrological sections:

**Rule S1 — Proximity = Scope:** Text INSIDE a pool acts on that pool; text OUTSIDE governs a larger frame. A label sitting in the pool describes the pool's contents. A paragraph floating above multiple pools describes the protocol governing all of them. This is SPATIAL SCOPING — where the text physically sits determines what it governs.

**Rule S2 — Vertical = Temporal:** Column text beside pipes reads TOP = EARLIER, BOTTOM = LATER. Vertical position encodes temporal sequence. This mirrors the astrological section's concentric-ring temporal hierarchy, but translated into linear vertical space.

**Rule S3 — Cascade = Flow:** Upper pools feed into lower pools through visible tubes. Material moves DOWNWARD through progressive purification stages. This is GRAVITY-DRIVEN FLOW — the simplest, most reliable engineering principle. Distillation runs downhill.

## The Control Law — Fixed-Point Convergence

The bath section implements a single, universal CONTROL LAW that governs every purification stage:

```
1. CIRCULATE (qokeedy) — pass material through purification cycle
2. CLAMP (chckhy) — test if output has changed since last cycle
3. If CHANGED: REPEAT from step 1
4. If UNCHANGED (fixed point reached): COMMIT (daiin) — lock the state
5. ROUTE to next stage or SEAL as final product
```

This is a FIXED-POINT CONVERGENCE ALGORITHM — repeat until the output stops changing, then commit. It is identical to:
- Modern iterative refinement in numerical analysis
- Fractional distillation (redistill until no further separation occurs)
- Recrystallization (redissolve and recrystallize until crystal purity stabilizes)
- Fixed-point iteration in functional programming

The control law appears on EVERY bath page. It is the universal operating principle — the bath section's equivalent of the herbal section's morphological grammar or the astrological section's planetary hierarchy.

## Domain-Shifted Morphology

The bath section uses the SAME VML morphemes as the herbal and astrological sections, but with domain-shifted frequencies:

| Morpheme | Herbal Meaning | Astrological Meaning | **Bath Meaning** |
|----------|---------------|---------------------|-----------------|
| qo- | Retort cycling | Calendar extraction | **CIRCULATION COMMAND** (dominant) |
| shedy | Infuse-stabilize | Temporal settlement | **SETTLE PHASE** (work↔settle oscillation) |
| chckhy | Valve/clamp | Temporal valve | **CONVERGENCE TEST** (has output stabilized?) |
| daiin | Product verification | Specification verification | **COMMIT** (lock purified state) |
| sal/sar | Salt crystallization | Temporal crystallization | **PURITY TEST** (crystals form when pure) |
| -edy | Essence-fixed | Scheduled essence-fixed | **FRACTION LOCKED** (purified fraction sealed) |
| ol | Fluid medium | Fluid medium | **FLUID PATH** (pipe/channel contents) |

**The critical shift:** In the herbal section, qo- appeared occasionally as retort cycling. In the bath section, qo- DOMINATES — typically 40-60% of all tokens on any given page. The bath section is a CIRCULATION ENGINE. Everything circulates.

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# PART I — FOLIO F75R: THE NETWORK INITIALIZER
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F75R — DISTRIBUTED PURIFICATION NETWORK — OPENING BATH

## Visual Description

Large tiered pool system with multiple nude female figures (nymphs) immersed in or moving between interconnected basins. Pools arranged in a hierarchical cascade — upper pools feed through visible tubes/pipes into lower pools. At least 10 nymph figures visible, each positioned at a specific node in the network. Text labels appear inside pools, along connecting pipes, and in paragraph blocks above the diagram. Some nymphs hold objects or reach toward pipe connections.

**What you see:** A PLUMBING SCHEMATIC. Not a scene of bathing — a technical diagram showing fluid flow through a multi-chamber purification system. Each pool is a stage; each nymph marks a process state; each pipe carries material between stages.

## Scale and Significance

F75r is the LARGEST single page in the bath section — 46 paragraphs of protocol text. Compare:
- Herbal folios: typically 3-8 paragraphs
- Astrological f58r (the specification): 40 paragraphs
- **F75r: 46 paragraphs** — the DENSEST protocol page in the manuscript

This density establishes f75r as the NETWORK INITIALIZER — the page that defines the entire bath system's architecture and control law, just as f58r defined the astrological system's temporal architecture.

## The {figure} Block Structure

F75r introduces a notation unique to the bath section: the `{figure}` block. Each paragraph contains TWO halves separated by `{figure}`:

```
LEFT TEXT — {figure} — RIGHT TEXT
```

The {figure} marks where a NYMPH is positioned in the diagram. The LEFT text = the PROTOCOL COMMAND (what to do). The RIGHT text = the LOCAL SUBROUTINE (what happens at that nymph's node). This is CALL-AND-RESPONSE architecture: the master protocol CALLS an operation; the local node RESPONDS with its specific execution.

This echoes f65v's stem-divided couplets (operation → {stem} → result) from the astrological section. The manuscript reuses the same LEFT/RIGHT encoding strategy across sections.

## Paragraph-by-Paragraph Deep Dive — The 46-Line Master Protocol

### Opening Block (P.1–P.5): SYSTEM BOOT

**P.1:** `f!!!chedykary — {figure} — okeey.qokar.shykchedy.qokar.shedy`

- LEFT: `f!!!chedykary` — The F-ATOM (formative/vegetative) with `!!!` emphasis markers. Venus's growth principle is the FIRST WORD of the bath section. The `!!!` notation (appearing as decorated initial in the manuscript) marks this as a SECTION HEADER — the formative growth principle OPENS the purification system.
- RIGHT: `okeey.qokar.shykchedy.qokar.shedy` — Phase-essence-active + EXTRACT-root (×2) + vigorous-flow-volatile + SETTLE.
- **TRANSLATION:** "GROWTH PRINCIPLE [opens section] → Phase essence, EXTRACT to root, vigorously flow the volatile, EXTRACT to root again, SETTLE."
- **MEANING:** The very first operation is: EXTRACT, FLOW, EXTRACT, SETTLE. This is the CONTROL LAW stated immediately — circulate, extract, settle. The entire 46-paragraph protocol begins by declaring its operating principle in the first line.
- **CRITICAL:** `qokar` appears TWICE. The doubled extraction-to-root is the control law's core: extract, check, extract again. If it comes out the same both times, you've reached convergence.

**P.2:** `dain.shey.ly — {figure} — ssheol.qolchedy.chedykar.chekeedy.rar`

- LEFT: `dain` = fix-complete = FIRST CHECKPOINT. `shey` = transition-essence-active. `ly` = layer-active.
- RIGHT: `ssheol` = intensified-transition-heat-fluid. `qolchedy` = transmute-layer-volatile-fixed. `chedykar` = volatile-fix-body-root. `chekeedy` = volatile-essence-body-essence-fixed. `rar` = rotation-root.
- **TRANSLATION:** "CHECKPOINT: transitioned essence layer → Intensified fluid transition, transmute volatile layer, volatile fixed at body-root, volatile essence contained and fixed, rotated at root."
- **MEANING:** The SECOND paragraph issues the FIRST dain (completion checkpoint) — before ANY work is done, the system VERIFIES its starting state. You check your equipment before turning it on. Then the local subroutine describes the volatile processing at this node: intensify, transmute, fix at root.

**P.3:** `qokain.cham — {figure} — okchey.qey.keiin.sheeky.ltain.olkar.or`

- LEFT: `qokain` = extract-complete. `cham` = channel-union. The extraction reaches COMPLETION and the product enters the CHANNEL UNION — the main pipeline.
- RIGHT: `okchey` = phase-volatile-active. `keiin` = body-contain-cycle. `sheeky` = transition-essence-body-active. `ltain` = layer-energy-complete. `olkar` = fluid-body-root.
- **TRANSLATION:** "EXTRACT COMPLETE → channel union → Phase volatile, contain through cycle, transition essence body, layer energy to completion, fluid at body root."
- **MEANING:** The third node completes its extraction and feeds into the main channel. The local subroutine cycles the volatile through phase-containment until the layer's energy is complete.

**P.4:** `dackhy.lkamo — {figure} — ykeey.lshey.kal.dy.shey.ok.shey.qokeedy`

- LEFT: `dackhy` = fix-VALVE. `lkamo` = layer-body-union-heat. The valve is FIXED (set) at the layer-body-union point.
- RIGHT: ends with `qokeedy` — the CORE CIRCULATION COMMAND (extract-essence-energy-fixed).
- **TRANSLATION:** "FIX VALVE at layer-body-union → Moist essence active, layer transition, contain fixed, transition, phase, transition, CIRCULATE."
- **MEANING:** The fourth node SETS A VALVE and then runs the core circulation command. This is the first appearance of `qokeedy` in the bath section proper — the command that will appear hundreds of times across the remaining 19 folios.

**P.5:** `sheykar.shey — {figure} — ckhey.r.ain.ol.olsheedy.qoreey.qoky`

- LEFT: `sheykar` = transition-essence-body-root. `shey` = transition active.
- RIGHT: `ckhey` = CKH VALVE-active. `ain` = complete. `olsheedy` = fluid-transition-essence-fixed. `qoreey` = transmute-rotation-essence-active. `qoky` = extract active.
- **TRANSLATION:** "Transition essence to root → VALVE active, complete, fluid transition fixed, transmute-rotate essence, extract."
- **MEANING:** The fifth node activates its valve and runs a local extraction. The CKH valve at P.5 echoes the valve set at P.4 — TWO VALVE OPERATIONS in the first five paragraphs. The system is establishing its flow-control infrastructure before the main purification begins.

### The p!!! Headers — Section Markers Within the Protocol

Seven paragraphs begin with `p!!!` (P.1, P.6, P.7, P.13, P.17, P.23, P.27, P.32): these are DECORATED INITIALS in the manuscript that mark SUB-SECTION HEADERS within the 46-paragraph protocol. The p!!! paragraphs divide the protocol into approximately 7 phases:

| Phase | Paragraphs | Header Token | Function |
|-------|-----------|-------------|----------|
| 1 | P.1–P.5 | f!!!chedykary | **BOOT** — system initialization with growth principle |
| 2 | P.6–P.12 | p!!!cheykeear / p!!!chedy | **PRIME** — extraction priming, first valve circuits |
| 3 | P.13–P.16 | p!!!chedy.keedy | **MULTIPLY** — quadruple extraction cascade |
| 4 | P.17–P.22 | p!!!chedar | **CHANNEL** — conduit routing and salt testing |
| 5 | P.23–P.26 | p!!!chey.kshey | **TEST** — salt-body test, convergence approach |
| 6 | P.27–P.31 | p!!!dalshor | **INTENSIFY** — doubled operations, accelerating cycles |
| 7 | P.32–P.46 | p!!!olshy | **CONVERGE** — final convergence cascade |

### Phase 3: The Quadruple Extraction (P.13) — The Control Law Made Visible

**P.13:** `p!!!chedy.keedy.qokedy — {figure} — qokedy.qokedy.qokedy.qokain.olshedy`

This is the most structurally significant paragraph in the bath section. The RIGHT side reads:

`qokedy.qokedy.qokedy.qokain.olshedy`

= EXTRACT-fixed. EXTRACT-fixed. EXTRACT-fixed. EXTRACT-COMPLETE. Fluid-settle.

**FOUR CONSECUTIVE EXTRACTIONS** followed by completion and settling. The control law is stated RAW: extract, extract, extract, extract until COMPLETE, then settle. This is ITERATION — the same operation repeated until convergence is declared.

**Why four?** In fractional distillation, four redistillations typically achieves ~95% separation. In recrystallization, four cycles typically yields pharmaceutical-grade purity. The number is not arbitrary — it reflects empirical practice.

### Phase 5: The Salt Test (P.25) — Convergence Detection

**P.25:** `sain.shckhel.qokeedy.shydy — {figure} — qokeedy.lchedy.ram`

- `sain` = salt-complete → "salt test PASSED"
- `shckhel` = vigorous-flow-CKH-VALVE-layer → "vigorous flow through valve at layer"
- `qokeedy` = core circulation (×2, both left and right)
- `ram` = rotation-union → "rotation reaches union"

**TRANSLATION:** "SALT TEST PASSED — vigorous valve flow at layer, circulate, vigorous settle → Circulate again at layer, ROTATION REACHES UNION."

**MEANING:** The salt test (crystallization purity test) determines convergence. When salt crystals form consistently (sain = salt complete), the material has reached FIXED-POINT PURITY. The `ram` (rotation-union) at the end signifies that the circular process has CLOSED — rotation reached its union point = the cycle is done.

### Phase 6: Doubled Operations (P.34–P.36) — Acceleration Before Convergence

**P.34:** `solkedy.okal.dar.oty.otar.otar.ol.kain.oltedy`
- `otar.otar` = DOUBLED temporal-root → "temporal root stated TWICE"
- This is the SAME doubling pattern from f58r P.5 in the astrological specification!
- **MEANING:** At the intensification phase, the temporal root is doubled — time pressure INCREASES. The system accelerates toward convergence.

**P.35:** `q.kain.sheety.qokain.dar.dar.shedy.qoked.oldy`
- `dar.dar` = DOUBLED fix-root → "fixation at root stated TWICE"
- **MEANING:** Fixation is also doubled. Both time (otar.otar) and fixation (dar.dar) are doubled in the intensification phase. The system is being DRIVEN toward its fixed point.

**P.36:** `rol.keedy.qokeedy.qok*.okar.otar.dar.dardy`
- `otar.dar.dardy` = temporal-root + fix-root + fix-root-fixed
- **THREE FIXATIONS** closing the paragraph → TRIPLE LOCK at the intensification peak

### Phase 7: The Convergence Cascade (P.37–P.38) — The Climax

**P.37:** `qokedy.dy.sheety.qokedy.qokeedy.qokeeedy.lol`
- `qokedy → qokeedy → qokeeedy` = extract-fixed → extract-DOUBLE-E-fixed → extract-**TRIPLE-E**-fixed
- **ESCALATING EXTRACTION:** Each successive extraction command carries MORE ESSENCE:
  - qokedy = single-e extraction
  - qokeedy = double-e extraction
  - qokeeedy = TRIPLE-E extraction
- The extractions INTENSIFY with each pass — more essence is extracted with each cycle as the material approaches purity
- **THIS IS THE BATH SECTION'S FIRST TRIPLE-E TOKEN** — appearing at the climax of the convergence cascade

**P.38:** `qoteedy.qokeedy.qokedy.qokedy.qokeedy.ldy`
- FIVE consecutive qo- extraction commands in a single paragraph
- Pattern: transmute-double-E → extract-double-E → extract-single-E → extract-single-E → extract-double-E
- The intensity OSCILLATES: high → high → low → low → high
- This is DAMPED OSCILLATION — the system is ringing down to its final state, oscillating with decreasing amplitude until it settles at the fixed point

### Closing Block (P.44–P.46): SYSTEM FINALIZATION

**P.44:** `dchedy.rain.okedy.qokedy.otedy.okoldy.otar.otiim.olair.eedar.dy`
- `rain` = rotation-complete → "rotation COMPLETE"
- `otar.otiim.olair` = temporal-root + temporal-extended-cycle + fluid-complete-root
- `eedar` = essence-energy-fix-root → "essence energy fixed at root"
- **MEANING:** The rotation is DECLARED COMPLETE. Extended temporal cycling at fluid root. All essence energy is FIXED AT ROOT. The system has converged.

**P.45:** `sshedy.shckhy.qokey.okedy.rorol.oty.otedy.qotedy.otedy.okaiin`
- `shckhy` = vigorous-flow-CKH-VALVE → FINAL VALVE CHECK
- `rorol` = rotation-rotation-fluid → DOUBLED ROTATION at fluid
- `okaiin` = phase-double-life-cycle → FULL PHASE CYCLE COMPLETE
- **MEANING:** Final valve check. Doubled rotation confirms the fluid is stable. The full phase cycle is declared complete. The network's convergence has been VERIFIED.

**P.46:** `qokey.qokedy.sheol.qokedy.deiin.shedy.otolchedy.olor`
- `deiin` = fix-extended-cycle → EXTENDED COMPLETION
- `otolchedy` = temporal-fluid-volatile-fixed → "timed fluid volatile locked"
- `olor` = fluid-rotation → the final output is a ROTATING FLUID
- **MEANING:** Final extraction, final settling, extended completion declared, timed fluid volatile locked. The output is a rotating fluid = a DISTILLATE in circulation. The purified product exits as a stable, circulating fluid.

## F75r — What It Teaches About the Bath Section

F75r establishes EVERYTHING the practitioner needs to know:

1. **The control law:** Circulate → Test → Repeat or Commit (stated in P.1, demonstrated in P.13)
2. **The valve infrastructure:** CKH valves set in the first five paragraphs, checked throughout
3. **The convergence method:** Salt test (P.25) detects when purity stabilizes
4. **The intensification protocol:** Doubled operations (P.34-36) accelerate convergence
5. **The oscillation pattern:** Extract-settle-extract-settle rhythms drive material to fixed point
6. **The escalation hierarchy:** Single-E → Double-E → Triple-E extraction at climax (P.37)
7. **The output format:** Purified product exits as stable rotating fluid (P.46)

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# PART II — FOLIO F75V: THE SCALE BRIDGE
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F75V — HIERARCHICAL FLOW CONTROLLER — MICROCHANNEL TO RESERVOIR

## Visual Description

Complex multi-level bath system with TWO SCALES of pools: small upper microchannels (~10) feeding into a larger lower reservoir containing ~19 nymph figures. Visible bridge connections between the two scales. Text organized in pipe-column labels (K-series) and pool-node labels (L-series). The page shows explicit SCALE TRANSITION — small batches being combined into a larger unified bath.

**What you see:** A SCALE-UP DIAGRAM. The upper microchannels are TEST BATCHES — small quantities processed individually. The lower reservoir is the PRODUCTION BATCH — the combined output of all successful test batches. This is standard laboratory-to-production scale-up: verify at small scale, then combine into large scale.

## The Pipe Labels (K-series) — Single-Character Conduit Codes

F75v introduces the K-series labels — SINGLE-CHARACTER codes placed along pipes:

| Label | Character | VML | Conduit State |
|-------|-----------|-----|--------------|
| K.1 | s | Salt/flowing | **Salt-flowing conduit** — crystallizing material in transit |
| K.2 | l | Layer/structure | **Layered conduit** — stratified material flowing |
| K.3 | l | Layer/structure | **Layered conduit** (REPEAT) |
| K.4 | o | Heat/activate | **Heated conduit** — material under thermal activation |
| K.5 | r | Rotation/source | **Rotating conduit** — material in circular flow |

**SINGLE-CHARACTER LABELS ARE MAXIMALLY COMPRESSED INSTRUCTIONS.** Where the herbal section uses 3-10 character tokens and the astrological section uses 4-12 character nymph labels, the bath section's pipe labels reduce to SINGLE CHARACTERS. This is not abbreviation — it is CONTEXT-DEPENDENT COMPRESSION. A pipe can only be in one state at a time; one character suffices to describe it.

**The sequence s → l → l → o → r encodes the PIPE STATE PROGRESSION:**
Salt-flowing → Layered → Layered → Heated → Rotating

Material enters the pipe as salt-flowing (crystallizing), passes through TWO layers of stratification, is heated, then enters rotation. This five-step pipe-state sequence IS the conduit's purification protocol — applied to the material AS IT FLOWS between stages.

## The Pool Labels (L-series) — Node State Descriptors

F75v has TWO tiers of pool labels: L1 (20 microchannel nodes) and L2 (4 reservoir nodes).

### L1 — The 20 Microchannel Node States

| # | Label | VML | Node Character |
|---|-------|-----|---------------|
| L1.1 | oksho | Phase-transition-heat | **Phase-heated transition** |
| L1.2 | saral | Salt-root-structure | **Crystalline structure at root** |
| L1.3 | dokol | Fix-phase-fluid | **Fixed phased fluid** |
| L1.4 | darol | Fix-root-fluid | **Fixed fluid at root** |
| L1.5 | daldy | Fix-structure-fixed | **DOUBLE-FIXED structure** |
| L1.6 | dalshd | Fix-structure-transition | **Fixed structure transitioning** |
| L1.7 | dalkar | Fix-structure-body-root | **Fixed structure at body root** |
| L1.8 | qokal | Extract-structure | **EXTRACTION NODE** |
| L1.9 | dla | Fix-layer | **Fixed layer** |
| L1.10 | ory | Heat-rotation-active | **Heated rotation active** |
| L1.11 | oty | Temporal-active | **TIMED active** |
| L1.12 | lchy | Layer-volatile-active | **Layered volatile active** |
| L1.13 | dary | Fix-root-active | **Fixed root active** |
| L1.14 | dal | Fix-structure | **Fixed structure** (bare) |
| L1.15 | daldy | Fix-structure-fixed | **DOUBLE-FIXED** (REPEAT of L1.5) |
| L1.16 | qoted | Transmute-heat-essence-fix | **Transmuted heated essence fixed** |
| L1.17 | rkal | Rotation-body-structure | **Rotating body structure** |
| L1.18 | ykedy | Moist-body-essence-fixed | **Moist body essence fixed** |
| L1.19 | olkchy | Fluid-body-volatile-active | **Fluid body volatile active** |
| L1.20 | otoly | Temporal-fluid-active | **Timed fluid active** |

### L1 Pattern Analysis

**D- (FIX) DOMINANCE:** 11 of 20 labels begin with d- (fix/stabilize) or contain dal- (fix-structure). The microchannels are FIXING NODES — their primary function is to LOCK material into stable states. This confirms the bath section's role as PURIFICATION: material enters fluid, exits fixed.

**L1.5 AND L1.15 ARE IDENTICAL: `daldy`.** Two microchannels share the same state: double-fixed structure. This means two separate nodes in the network have CONVERGED to the same state — they are producing identical output. When multiple independent channels produce the same result, the result is VALIDATED BY REDUNDANCY.

**L1.8 = `qokal` — THE EXTRACTION NODE.** One and only one microchannel is labeled with qo- (extract). This is the EXTRACTION POINT — the node where material is pulled from the microchannel network into the reservoir system. All other nodes fix and stabilize; this one EXTRACTS.

**L1.11 = `oty` — THE TEMPORAL NODE.** One node is purely temporal-active. This is the TIMER — the node that tracks elapsed time without performing any chemical operation. A clock node in a processing network.

**L1.20 = `otoly` — THE EXIT NODE.** The last microchannel label is temporal-fluid-active. Compare f67r2 C.12 `otoldos` from the astrological master calendar — the same ot-ol compound. The exit node carries temporal-fluid: TIMED FLUID ready for transfer. This is the microchannel's FINAL PRODUCT: fluid that has been timed (processed for the correct duration) and is actively flowing toward the reservoir.

### L2 — The 4 Reservoir Node States

| # | Label | VML | Node Character |
|---|-------|-----|---------------|
| L2.1 | otal·opal | Temporal-structure + Expand-project-structure | **Timed structure EXPANDED** |
| L2.2 | okeey·lol | Phase-essence-active + Layer-fluid | **Phased essence in layered fluid** |
| L2.3 | olol | Fluid-fluid | **PURE FLUID** (doubled) |
| L2.4 | ytedy | Moist-energy-essence-fixed | **Moist energy essence LOCKED** |

**L2.1 = `otal·opal` — TIMED AND EXPANDED.** The reservoir's first node combines TEMPORAL (from microchannels) with EXPANDED (scale-up). This is the BRIDGE NODE: time-controlled material from the microchannels is expanded to production scale.

**L2.3 = `olol` — DOUBLED FLUID.** ol-ol = fluid-fluid. The reservoir's third node is PURE FLUID — fluid that is nothing but fluid. All solids have been removed, all volatiles have been captured. What remains is doubly-confirmed fluid medium. This is the PURIFIED PRODUCT.

**L2.4 = `ytedy` — THE FINAL STATE.** Moist-energy-essence-FIXED. The reservoir's output is moist (water-based), energized, essence-concentrated, and FIXED. This is the pharmaceutical-grade input material that the Pharmaceutical section's recipes will use.

## Protocol Analysis — Selected Critical Paragraphs

### P.1: The Opening with Fire Seal

**P.1:** `p!!!chedar.opchedy.qokedy.opchedy.qopdy — dain.chetar.chcfhey.qotam`

- LEFT: expand-volatile-fixed → extract-fixed → expand-volatile-fixed → transmute-fluid-fixed
- RIGHT: `chcfhey` = channel-**FIRE SEAL**-essence-active
- **THE FIRE SEAL IN THE BATH SECTION'S FIRST PARAGRAPH.** The cfh- fire seal that evolved through seven herbal quires, appeared in the astrological specification (f58r P.36), sat at the center of the red-ink master calendar (f67r2 Z.3), and marked specific degree-days on zodiac wheels — NOW appears in the FIRST PARAGRAPH of the bath section.
- `qotam` = transmute-heat-union → "transmuted heat into union"
- **MEANING:** The fire seal at the reservoir's opening declares: THE SCALE-UP PROCESS REQUIRES FIRE-SEALED CAUTION. Moving from test batches to production batches is DANGEROUS — thermal runaway is more likely at larger scale. The fire seal warns: proceed carefully.

### P.2: Double CKH Valve

**P.2:** `sor.sheky.qokain.okal.dal.olchedy — daiin.chckhey.lkar.chckhey.nom`

- RIGHT: `chckhey` appears TWICE → DOUBLE CKH VALVE
- `daiin` = FULL COMPLETION MARKER (not dain but daiin — doubled 'i' = extended verification)
- `nom` — a rare token, possibly "normal/nominal" or a status indicator
- **MEANING:** The second paragraph installs a DOUBLE VALVE checkpoint with FULL VERIFICATION. Two CKH valves in series = redundant flow control. The reservoir system requires DOUBLE the valve security of the microchannel system.

### P.13: The Doubled-QO Extraction

**P.13:** `qoqokeey.olkain.qolsheedy.qokeor.sheedy.qokal.or.chey.qokar.ol.aiin`

- `qoqokeey` = transmute-transmute-extract-essence-active → DOUBLED QO PREFIX
- `aiin` = double-life-cycle at the close
- **MEANING:** `qoqokeey` is a COMPOUND CIRCULATION — transmute WITHIN a transmutation. This is NESTED CYCLING: the outer cycle transmutes material that is ITSELF being transmuted in an inner cycle. Distillation of distillate. Purification of purified material. The bath system supports RECURSIVE OPERATIONS.

### P.22: The Terminal Checkpoint

**P.22:** `qokear.chedy.shckhy.dol.ycheedy.saino.ol.che.dy.qokar.otar.dal.daiin`

- `shckhy` = vigorous-flow-CKH-VALVE → valve under vigorous flow
- `saino` = salt-complete-heat → "salt test passed with heat"
- CLOSES with `otar.dal.daiin` = temporal-root + fix-structure + FULL COMPLETION
- **MEANING:** The terminal checkpoint: valve tested under vigorous flow, salt purity confirmed with heat, temporal root fixed into structure, FULL COMPLETION declared. This is the FINAL QUALITY GATE before material enters the next section.

### P.29: The Double-Double Checkpoint

**P.29:** `qotedy — {pond} — qokal.dain.dain.oqoky.daiin`

- `dain.dain` = DOUBLE completion marker
- `daiin` = FULL completion marker IMMEDIATELY AFTER the double dain
- **THREE COMPLETION MARKERS IN ONE PARAGRAPH:** dain + dain + daiin
- **MEANING:** The reservoir's internal checkpoint issues TRIPLE VERIFICATION. The reservoir demands MORE verification than the microchannels — consistent with the higher stakes of production-scale operation. If a test batch fails, you lose a small amount. If the production batch fails, you lose everything.

### The {pond} Structure — Reservoir Subroutines (P.24–P.34)

Paragraphs P.24 through P.34 use `{pond}` instead of `{figure}` — marking that these operations occur in the RESERVOIR rather than at individual nymph nodes. The pond paragraphs describe the reservoir's internal processing:

| Para | Key Feature | Reservoir Phase |
|------|-------------|----------------|
| P.24 | kolkedy.qokedy | Body-fluid extraction in reservoir |
| P.25 | okshey.qolkeey.leedy | Phase-shifted transmuted layered essence |
| P.26 | ykeechy.**qokeedy.daiin** | Moist body essence → CIRCULATION + VERIFIED |
| P.27 | oteey.qolchey.qokey | Temporal essence → transmute-channel → extract |
| P.28 | qol.dy.qokar.shey | Transmute → fix → extract-root → transition |

| P.30 | okal.sheedy.qoteedy | Phase-structure settled, transmuted essence fixed |
| P.31 | ykeedy.**qokain.otain** | Moist essence → EXTRACT COMPLETE + TEMPORAL COMPLETE |
| P.32 | octhey.shedy.**otol.checkhy** | Conduit active → settle → temporal-fluid + **VALVE** |
| P.33 | okeshey.olkedy.olkedy | Phase-transition, fluid-fixed (×2) |
| P.34 | qokey.olchedy.**otey.orol** | Extract → fluid-volatile-fixed → **TEMPORAL + HEAT-ROTATION** |

**P.26 = THE RESERVOIR'S CONVERGENCE POINT.** `qokeedy.daiin` = core circulation command + full completion. The reservoir reaches its own convergence — the production batch's purity has been verified.

**P.32 = THE RESERVOIR'S VALVE.** `checkhy` = volatile-CKH-VALVE. The reservoir has its OWN valve, distinct from the microchannel valves. The scale-up system has INDEPENDENT flow control at each scale.

**P.34 = THE RESERVOIR'S EXIT.** `otey.orol` = temporal-essence-active + heat-rotation-fluid. The reservoir's output is temporally-active essence in heated rotating fluid — a LIVE DISTILLATE ready for pharmaceutical use.

**The pattern is clear:** as scale INCREASES, safety INTENSIFIES. More valves, more checkpoints, fire seals, nested operations, multiple verification — all appear at the LARGER scale. The bath section teaches: purification at test scale is routine; purification at production scale is dangerous.

# PART III — FOLIO F76R: THE STABILITY DOCTRINE
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F76R — STABILITY DOCTRINE — CONTROL THEORY REFERENCE

## Visual Description

Dense text page with pool/bath diagram. Long paragraph blocks dominate the visual field — text volume EXCEEDS the diagram for the first time in the bath section. Nymph figures present but subordinate to text. Multiple repetition patterns visible in the EVA text (qokeedy, qokedy, shedy cycling). Single-character pool/node labels (s, d, q, l, k, s) placed at intervals throughout.

**What you see:** A REFERENCE MANUAL PAGE. This is not primarily an operational diagram — it is the CONTROL THEORY SPECIFICATION. The text DEFINES the convergence criteria that all subsequent bath operations must satisfy. The repeated morpheme patterns (qokeedy/shedy cycling) ARE the control law written out explicitly: "keep cycling extraction and infusion until the output stabilizes."

## Scale and Significance

F76r is the CONTROL THEORY PAGE — it formalizes what f75r demonstrated. Where f75r showed the control law IN ACTION (through 46 paragraphs of operational protocol), f76r DEFINES the control law AS LAW (through 47 paragraphs of specification text).

**47 R-series text blocks.** The R- prefix (vs. f75r's P- prefix) signals a different text TYPE: these are RULES, not protocols. Protocols tell you what to do; rules tell you what MUST be true.

## The Section Labels — Element Markers in the Network

F76r uses single-character labels placed at specific structural positions within the text:

| Position | Label | VML | Network Node |
|----------|-------|-----|-------------|
| R.4 | s | Salt | **SALT STATION** — crystallization test point |
| R.6 | d | Fix | **FIXATION STATION** — stabilization test point |
| R.8 | q | Extract | **EXTRACTION STATION** — circulation test point |
| R.11 | s | Salt | **SALT STATION** (repeat) |
| R.14 | o | Heat | **HEAT STATION** — thermal activation point |
| R.17 | l | Layer | **LAYER STATION** — stratification test point |
| R.21 | k | Body/contain | **CONTAINMENT STATION** — body-containment test point |
| R.24 | k | Body/contain | **CONTAINMENT STATION** (repeat) |
| R.29 | s | Salt | **SALT STATION** (third) |

**THE NETWORK ALPHABET: s-d-q-s-o-l-k-k-s**

Nine single-character labels using SIX VML categories:
- s (salt) appears THREE TIMES — salt testing is the most frequent checkpoint
- k (contain) appears TWICE — containment requires redundant verification
- d, q, o, l each appear ONCE — fixation, extraction, heat, layering each tested once

This is the MINIMUM VIABLE TEST SUITE — the smallest set of tests that verifies a complete purification cycle. To confirm purity, you must test: crystallization (s×3), containment (k×2), fixation (d), extraction (q), heat response (o), and stratification (l). The three salt tests at beginning, middle, and end bracket the entire cycle — salt crystallization is the GOLD STANDARD of purity.

## Critical Rule Paragraphs — Selected Analysis

### R.1: The Opening Specification

**R.1:** `p!!!otchokar.chcphdy.opshdy.qolp.chcphy.chcphdy.opshey.qofshy.opchdy.sain.asy`

- `p!!!otchokar` = PROJECT-TEMPORAL-VOLATILE-HEAT-ROOT — the specification opens with the FULL OPERATIONAL CHAIN: time→volatile→heat→root. Every element of the purification process is invoked in the first token.
- THREE `chcph-` tokens (chcphdy, chcphy, chcphdy) — `cph` is a RARE MORPHEME found almost exclusively in the bath section. It may encode a CONDUIT-PROJECTION-HEAT compound — the specific physical apparatus (condenser tube) through which volatile projections pass under heat.
- THREE `op-` tokens (opshdy, opshey, opchdy) — EXPANSION/PROJECTION commands, also triple-stated.
- CLOSES with `sain` (salt-complete) — the specification's first paragraph ends by DECLARING PURITY.
- **MEANING:** "PROJECT the full temporal-volatile-heat-root cycle: channel-project-heat the volatile, expand the projection, circulate through layers, channel-project-heat again, expand the transition, circulate through formative vigorous flow, expand the volatile. Salt test PASSED."
- **CRITICAL:** The triple cph- and triple op- establish that CONDUIT PHYSICS is central to the specification. The bath section is about CONDUITS — the physical tubes through which material flows.

### R.5: The Triple-E Salt Token

**R.5:** `soleeedy.qokeedy.qopchedy.qokeey.kol.shedy.qokedy.sheey.okeer.al.al.chedainda`

- `soleeedy` = SALT-FLUID-**TRIPLE-E**-FIXED — **TRIPLE-E IN A SALT TOKEN.**
- This is the bath section's SPECIFICATION of triple-e intensity. Where f75r P.37 demonstrated triple-e as an operational event (qokeeedy), f76r R.5 DEFINES triple-e as a salt property (soleeedy).
- `al.al` = structure-structure — DOUBLED STRUCTURE
- `chedainda` = volatile-DAIIN-fix — volatile material that VERIFIES (daiin) and fixes in a single compound token.
- **MEANING:** "Salt flowing at TRIPLE INTENSITY → extract essence fixed → transmute fluid volatile → extract essence active → contain in fluid → settle → extract fixed → transition essence active → phase essence energy → structure DOUBLED → volatile verified-and-fixed."
- **TEACHING:** Triple-e is not just high intensity — it is a SALT PROPERTY. When salt crystallizes at triple-e concentration, the purification has reached its theoretical maximum. This is the specification of PHARMACEUTICAL-GRADE PURITY.

### R.8: The Central Valve Specification

**R.8:** `qotedshedy.qorain.oteedy.chedy.ol.chdy.raiiin.chekain.dain.chckhy.sal.oty`

- `raiiin` = rotation-**TRIPLE-I** (extended temporal cycling)
- `dain.chckhy.sal.oty` = CHECKPOINT → VALVE → SALT → TEMPORAL-ACTIVE
- **MEANING:** The rule specifies: after extended rotation cycling (triple-i), issue a CHECKPOINT, test the VALVE, run a SALT TEST, then activate the temporal cycle. This is the CENTRAL INTERLOCK: rotation → verify → valve → salt → time.
- The triple-i (`raiiin`) in the bath section's specification echoes the triple-i in astrological labels (okaiiin) — extended cycling operates identically across domains.

### R.13: The Embedded Triple-E

**R.13:** `chey.chckh.sheoqeeey.chol.lkain.shedy.qokeedy.okain.chedy.okeed.qokaloro`

- `sheoqeeey` = transition-heat-transmute-**TRIPLE-E**-active — `qeee` = transmute at triple-E
- `chckh` = CKH valve (bare, without suffix) — valve in SPECIFICATION mode (defining, not operating)
- `qokaloro` = extract-structure-fluid-rotation-heat — a compound token describing the FULL EXTRACTION PATHWAY
- **MEANING:** The rule specifies that when the valve (chckh) encounters a transition at triple-E intensity (sheoqeeey), the volatile is heated to fluid, layered to containment, settled, circulated, phased to completion, volatile fixed, phased to essence energy, then EXTRACTED through the full structural-fluid-rotation-heat pathway. This is a COMPLETE PROCESS SPECIFICATION for handling peak-intensity material.

### R.16: The Triple-E Fluid Token

**R.16:** `qokchsdy.okeey.lchedy.qo.olain.ot.shedy.qotaly.dar.sain.shedy.oleeed`

- `oleeed` = FLUID-**TRIPLE-E**-FIXED — fluid at triple-E intensity, fixed
- `sain` = salt complete (AGAIN — third salt test in the specification)
- `dar.sain.shedy.oleeed` = fix-root → salt-complete → settle → fluid-TRIPLE-E-fixed
- **MEANING:** After fixation at root, after salt test passes, after settling, the fluid reaches TRIPLE-E concentration and is FIXED. This is the ENDPOINT SPECIFICATION: what the purified product looks like when done.

### R.22: The Extraction-Settle Oscillation Rule

**R.22:** `qokar.shedy.shedy.qokar.shedy.qokain.dar.shey.lshcthy.okar.okain.ydaiiny`

- `qokar.shedy.shedy.qokar.shedy` = EXTRACT-SETTLE-SETTLE-EXTRACT-SETTLE
- The OSCILLATION PATTERN is spelled out EXPLICITLY: extract, settle, settle, extract, settle
- TWO settles between extractions = more settling time than extraction time
- `ydaiiny` = moist-DAIIN-active — moistened FULL VERIFICATION at the close
- **MEANING:** "Extract to root → settle → settle → extract to root → settle → extraction COMPLETE → fix at root → transition active → layer through conduit → phase at root → phase complete → VERIFIED-AND-ACTIVE."
- **TEACHING:** The extraction-settle ratio is 2:3 (two extractions per three settles). The system spends MORE TIME SETTLING than extracting. Patience yields purity. This matches empirical distillation practice — most of the time is WAITING for fractions to separate.

### R.33: The Terminal Checkpoint

**R.33:** `dain.chey.lsh.daiin.chey`

- FIVE TOKENS ONLY — the shortest rule in the specification
- `dain` → `daiin` — SIMPLE checkpoint followed by FULL verification
- `chey` appears TWICE — volatile-essence-active bookends both checkpoints
- **MEANING:** "CHECKPOINT. Volatile active. Layer vigorous. FULL VERIFICATION. Volatile active."
- **TEACHING:** The terminal checkpoint is MINIMALLY STATED. After 32 complex rules, the specification REDUCES to: check, verify, done. Complexity converges to simplicity. This echoes the convergence algorithm itself — complexity reduces until the output is simple enough to state in five tokens.

### R.41: The F-Atom Return

**R.41:** `f!!!chedy.g.sal.dol.shdy.olkedy.qokaiin.otal.oory`

- `f!!!chedy` = FORMATIVE/VEGETATIVE with `!!!` emphasis — the F-ATOM RETURNS
- `g` = THE 'g' GLYPH (gradatio = stepwise change) — rare morpheme from Scorpio (f73r)
- `sal.dol` = salt + fix-fluid — salt crystallization from fixed fluid
- `otal` = temporal-structure — astrological scheduling morpheme IN the bath specification
- **MEANING:** "GROWTH PRINCIPLE with gradual stepwise change: salt from fixed fluid, fluid body extracted through extended cycle, timed structure, heated rotation active."
- **CRITICAL:** The f-atom opened f75r P.1 (the network initializer) and now appears in f76r R.41 (near the specification's close). The growth principle BRACKETS the first two bath folios: P.1 opens it, R.41 closes it. Venus's growth force governs the entire purification network.
- **THE 'g' GLYPH:** First encountered in Scorpio (f73r S1.11 `oteedyg`), now in the bath specification. The gradatio marker appears at structural transition points — Scorpio's deep transformation, and now the bath section's specification of how growth occurs GRADUALLY through iterative purification.

### R.43: The Extraction Cascade

**R.43:** `olsheed.qokedy.qokeedy.qokedy.lkedy.lsheedy.okar.shedy.otain`

- `qokedy.qokeedy.qokedy` = extract-single → extract-DOUBLE → extract-single
- PATTERN: low → HIGH → low — the same damped oscillation from f75r P.37-38
- CLOSES with `otain` = temporal-COMPLETE
- **MEANING:** The specification DEFINES the extraction cascade pattern: oscillation between intensity levels, converging to temporal completion.

## F76r — What It Teaches

F76r is the CONSTITUTION of the bath section — it defines the rules that all subsequent operations must obey:

1. **Triple-e as salt property** (R.5): Purity is defined by salt crystallization at triple-e intensity
2. **Oscillation ratios** (R.22): Extract:settle = 2:3, patience yields purity
3. **Central interlock** (R.8): Rotation → verify → valve → salt → time
4. **Conduit physics** (R.1): Triple cph- compounds = physical apparatus specification
5. **Convergence endpoint** (R.16): oleeed = fluid at triple-e, fixed = pharmaceutical grade
6. **Minimum test suite** (labels): s-d-q-s-o-l-k-k-s = the nine essential checkpoints
7. **Terminal simplicity** (R.33): Complex rules converge to five-token verification

# PART IV — FOLIO F76V: THE ENDURANCE RUN
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F76V — ENDURANCE CONVERGENCE RUN — EXTENDED CYCLING

## Visual Description

Bath diagram with sustained cycling patterns. Nymph figures in pools undergoing extended processing. Text shows very long repetitive cycling sequences — the longest sustained oscillation patterns in the bath section. Clamp tokens appear at regular intervals throughout.

**What you see:** An ENDURANCE TEST. Where f75r demonstrated the control law and f76r specified it, f76v RUNS it — for an extended duration. This is the STRESS TEST: can the system maintain convergence over many cycles? The answer is embedded in the text's structure.

## The Endurance Pattern — Sustained Oscillation Under Clamp Control

F76v's defining characteristic is SUSTAINED REPETITION. The text contains the longest unbroken cycling sequences in the bath section:

### P.13: The Double Triple-E Paragraph

**P.13:** `saiin.sheedy.qol.sheedy.okeeedy.qoteedy.chedy.qotedy.oleeedy.qoteedy.lo`

- `okeeedy` = phase-**TRIPLE-E**-fixed — triple-E in phase domain
- `oleeedy` = fluid-**TRIPLE-E**-fixed — triple-E in fluid domain
- **TWO TRIPLE-E TOKENS IN ONE PARAGRAPH** — phase triple-E AND fluid triple-E
- Both are DIFFERENT DOMAINS reaching the same intensity: the solid material (phase) and the liquid material (fluid) BOTH reach triple-E simultaneously
- `saiin` opens — salt extended-cycle = the SALT ENDURANCE TEST
- **MEANING:** "Salt extended-cycle: transition-settle, circulate, transition-settle, phase at TRIPLE INTENSITY, transmute-heat-double-E, volatile fixed, transmute-heat, fluid at TRIPLE INTENSITY, transmute-heat-double-E, layer."
- **TEACHING:** In the endurance run, BOTH phases of the material must reach triple-E independently. Convergence requires ALL fractions to achieve maximum intensity, not just one.

### P.14: The Maximum Density Paragraph

**P.14:** `qokeedy.qol.cheedy.otedy.cthedy.otedy.qoteedy.shcthedy.qoeekeedy.deedy`

- SIX extraction/transmutation commands in a single paragraph (qokeedy, qol, otedy×2, qoteedy, qoeekeedy)
- `qoeekeedy` = transmute-ENERGY-body-essence-energy-fixed — a FIVE-MORPHEME compound extraction
- `deedy` = fix-essence-energy-fixed — double-locked essence
- **MEANING:** This is the PEAK DENSITY paragraph — maximum operational throughput. Every token is an active command; there are no settle phases. Pure action. This occurs in the middle of the endurance run when the system is at MAXIMUM VELOCITY — all operators running simultaneously.

### P.19: The Double-Valve Paragraph

**P.19:** `orar.sheey.otar.shedy.otedy.checkhey.olchedy.checkhy.checkhy.lky`

- `checkhy.checkhy` = DOUBLED VALVE — two consecutive valve checks
- `orar` = heat-rotation-root — active rotation under heat
- `otar` = temporal-root — timed root process
- **MEANING:** After sustained high-intensity cycling, the system requires DOUBLE VALVE VERIFICATION. Single-valve checks suffice during normal operation; the endurance run demands double checking because sustained high intensity may cause valve fatigue. This is ENGINEERING PRUDENCE.

### P.20: The Triple-I Token

**P.20:** `dol.sheetey.qokedy.ol.checkhy.lshedy.qokeedy.cheedy.qokeedy.shl.loiiim`

- `loiiim` = layer-heat-**TRIPLE-I**-union — TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING reaching union
- Triple-i appeared in f76r R.8 as `raiiin` (rotation-triple-i). Now in f76v P.20, it is `loiiim` (layer-triple-i-union).
- **MEANING:** The endurance run produces triple-i cycling — the material's temporal phase extends to triple duration before reaching union. Extended cycling in the endurance run takes THREE TIMES longer than standard cycling.

### P.25: The Third Phase with F-Atom Connection

**P.25:** `p!!!sheoldy.opalshedy.qokshedy.qokedy.dor.shey.opchedy.dal.sofcham`

- `sofcham` = salt-heat-**F-ATOM**-channel-union — f-atom embedded in a SALT-CHANNEL compound
- `opalshedy` = expand-project-structure-settle — scale-up settling
- **MEANING:** The endurance run's third phase integrates the f-atom (Venus growth) into a salt-channel-union compound. Growth is UNIFIED with purification at the endurance stage — the material doesn't just get purer, it gets MORE POTENT.

### P.27: The Convergence Declaration

**P.27:** `daiin.shckhey.qokeedy.saiin.chek.ain.rain.o.kan.chlaiiin`

- `daiin` opens — FULL VERIFICATION
- `saiin` — salt extended-cycle PASSED
- `rain` — rotation COMPLETE
- `chlaiiin` = channel-layer-**TRIPLE-I**-cycle — SECOND triple-i in the endurance run
- **MEANING:** "VERIFIED. Vigorous valve active. Circulation fixed. Salt extended-test PASSED. Volatile complete. Rotation COMPLETE. Heat. Contained. Channel-layer TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLE."
- **TEACHING:** Convergence is declared when: (1) verification passes, (2) salt test passes, (3) rotation completes, and (4) triple-extended cycling is achieved through all channels. ALL FOUR CONDITIONS must be met simultaneously.

### P.31: The Maximum Extended Cycling

**P.31:** `sair.shekaiiin.shetsaiiin.shety.otey.okaiin.otedy.qotar.chedy`

- `shekaiiin` = transition-essence-body-**TRIPLE-I** — triple extended cycling of body essence
- `shetsaiiin` = transition-essence-temporal-salt-**TRIPLE-I** — triple extended cycling of temporal salt
- **TWO TRIPLE-I TOKENS IN ONE PARAGRAPH** — the endurance run's maximum intensity
- Both tokens apply triple-i to DIFFERENT SUBSTRATES: body-essence and temporal-salt
- `sair` opens — salt-complete-root = salt test at root PASSED
- **MEANING:** "Salt at root PASSED. Transition body-essence through TRIPLE-EXTENDED CYCLING. Transition temporal-salt through TRIPLE-EXTENDED CYCLING. Transition temporal. Temporal essence active. Phase double-cycle. Temporal essence fixed. Transmute-heat root. Volatile fixed."
- **TEACHING:** The endurance run's peak pushes TWO SEPARATE SUBSTRATES through triple-extended cycling simultaneously. This is PARALLEL ENDURANCE — testing whether multiple material fractions can sustain extreme duration simultaneously.

### P.33: The Terminal Salt-Valve

**P.33:** `sain.otaiin.shckhedy`

- THREE TOKENS ONLY — the endurance run's conclusion
- `sain` = salt COMPLETE
- `otaiin` = temporal double-life-cycle
- `shckhedy` = vigorous-flow-CKH-VALVE-fixed
- **MEANING:** "Salt PASSED. Temporal cycle COMPLETE. Vigorous valve FIXED."
- **TEACHING:** The endurance run ends with exactly three declarations: salt purity confirmed, temporal cycle complete, valve fixed. After 33 paragraphs of sustained cycling, the conclusion REDUCES to three words. Maximum complexity → minimum statement. This mirrors f76r R.33's five-token terminal checkpoint. Both the specification and the endurance run converge to BREVITY.

| p!!! section headers | **3** | Three endurance phases |
| Triple-E tokens | **2** (okeeedy, oleeedy) | Both domains simultaneously |
| Triple-I tokens | **4** (loiiim, chlaiiin, shekaiiin, shetsaiiin) | **HIGHEST TRIPLE-I DENSITY** |
| Double-valve checks | **1** (checkhy.checkhy) | Endurance safety |
| F-atom connection | **1** (sofcham) | Growth in purification |

## F76v — What It Teaches

F76v is the PROVING GROUND — it demonstrates that the system specified in f76r can sustain convergence over extended duration:

1. **Both phases must converge** (P.13): Phase triple-E AND fluid triple-E simultaneously
2. **Parallel endurance** (P.31): Multiple substrates through triple-extended cycling
3. **Valve fatigue management** (P.19): Double-valve checks during sustained operation
4. **Growth-purification unity** (P.25): F-atom integrates with salt channel at endurance stage
5. **Convergence criteria** (P.27): Verification + salt + rotation + triple-i must all pass
6. **Terminal brevity** (P.33): Three tokens close the run — complexity converges to simplicity

# PART V — FOLIO F77R: THE ROUTING CONTROLLER
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F77R — ROUTED BATHHOUSE CONTROLLER — CHANNEL LABELS

## Visual Description

Bath network with explicitly labeled channels/tubes. Each pipe connection bears a text label identifying it as a named route. Nymph figures at nodes. The diagram functions as EXECUTABLE PLUMBING — named channels that can be referenced by address. Top-tube route keys (~6 channel labels) visible.

**What you see:** A NETWORK ROUTER. F75r showed the network. F75v scaled it up. F76r specified its rules. F76v tested its endurance. Now f77r NAMES ITS CHANNELS — turning the network into an ADDRESSABLE SYSTEM where specific connections can be referenced by label.

## The Architectural Progression: f75r→f77r

| Folio | Function | Teaches |
|-------|----------|---------|
| f75r | Network initialization | HOW the system works |
| f75v | Scale-up | HOW MUCH the system handles |
| f76r | Stability specification | WHAT RULES govern the system |
| f76v | Endurance testing | HOW LONG the system runs |
| **f77r** | **Channel routing** | **WHERE material flows** |

F77r completes the system definition by answering the final question: WHERE does material go? With named channels, the practitioner can DIRECT material to specific destinations — not just "purify" but "purify through CHANNEL X to NODE Y."

## Protocol Analysis — Selected Critical Paragraphs

### P.1: The Opening Route Declaration

**P.1:** `p!!!aldarairal.qokol.chey.qopchedy.qopchedy.dylches.alkedy.laly`

- `p!!!aldarairal` = PROJECT-structure-fix-root-complete-rotation-structure — the opening token is the LONGEST SINGLE TOKEN in the bath section (14 characters). It encodes the ENTIRE ROUTING PATH in a single compound morpheme: structure→fixed→rooted→complete→rotated→structure. Material goes FROM structure THROUGH fixation, rooting, completion, rotation, BACK TO structure.
- `qopchedy.qopchedy` = DOUBLED transmute-fluid-volatile-fixed — the routing command is stated TWICE
- `alkedy.laly` = structure-body-fixed + layer-structure-active — destination specification
- **MEANING:** "DECLARE ROUTE [structure→fix→root→complete→rotate→structure]. Extract to fluid. Volatile active. Transmute-fluid-volatile TWICE. Fix volatile. Structure-body fixed. Layer-structure active."
- **TEACHING:** The route is a CYCLE — it starts at structure and returns to structure. All purification routes are CIRCULAR, just as all distillation is cyclic. The doubled qopchedy confirms the route is traversed TWICE before the material reaches its destination.

### P.4: The Double-Verification Route

**P.4:** `solteedy.qoteedy.qodeedy.chedaiin.chedy.shedaiin.sheolol.ched`

- `chedaiin` = volatile-DAIIN = volatile VERIFIED
- `shedaiin` = transition-DAIIN = transition VERIFIED
- **TWO DAIIN VERIFICATIONS** — both the volatile AND the transition are independently verified
- `qoteedy.qodeedy` = transmute-heat-double-E + transmute-fix-double-E — double-E in two different transmutation modes
- **MEANING:** On this route, both the volatile product and the transition process are independently verified before the route is declared complete. This is DUAL-CHANNEL VERIFICATION — the product AND the process must both pass.

### P.9: The Quintuple QO Cascade

**P.9:** `qoteedy.qoteedy.qokedy.sheed.qeey.saiin.sheety.qokeedy.lol`

- `qoteedy.qoteedy` = DOUBLED transmute-heat-double-E — two identical transmutations
- `qokedy` = extract-fixed
- `qeey` = a rare extraction-essence-active
- `qokeedy` = core circulation
- **FIVE QO- commands in ONE paragraph** — maximum extraction density, matching f75r P.38
- `saiin` at paragraph center — salt test embedded within the cascade
- CLOSES with `lol` = layer-fluid — the output is a LAYERED FLUID
- **MEANING:** This route runs five consecutive extraction/transmutation operations with a salt test at their center and produces a layered fluid output. The route IS the extraction cascade.

### P.11: The Quintuple QO — Pure Extraction Route

**P.11:** `qokeedy.lchey.lsheey.qokeedy.qokeedy.qokar.qokeey.laiin.chey`

- `qokeedy.qokeedy` = DOUBLED core circulation
- `qokar` = extract-root
- `qokeey` = extract-essence-active
- FIVE qo- commands AGAIN — this is the second quintuple-qo paragraph
- `laiin` = layer-double-life-cycle — extended layering cycle
- **MEANING:** This is a PURE EXTRACTION ROUTE — nothing but extraction commands plus layering. No fixation, no settling, no valves. Pure throughput. This route exists for material that has ALREADY been purified and just needs to be MOVED.

### P.16: The Terminal Route Seal

**P.16:** `daiin.dol.shar.cphey.lfcheal.shear.qolchy`

- `daiin` opens — FULL VERIFICATION
- `dol` = fix-fluid — fluid is FIXED
- `lfcheal` = layer-**F-ATOM**-volatile-structure — f-atom embedded in route seal!
- `qolchy` closes — transmute-layer-volatile-active
- **MEANING:** "VERIFIED. Fix fluid. Vigorous root. [Conduit active]. Layer GROWTH-volatile-structure. Transition root. Transmute-layer-volatile."
- **CRITICAL:** The f-atom appears in the ROUTE SEAL — the point where a channel is officially closed and its contents are committed. Venus's growth principle governs not just the material but the INFRASTRUCTURE. The channel itself carries growth.

### P.22: The Valve-Salt Route

**P.22:** `qokaiin.chckhey.saiin.qoklain.cheeky.lol`

- `chckhey` = CKH VALVE
- `saiin` = salt extended-cycle
- VALVE → SALT in direct sequence = the STANDARD INTERLOCK from f76r R.8
- **MEANING:** "Extract extended-cycle. VALVE. Salt extended-test. Extract layer-complete. Volatile essence active. Layer-fluid."
- **TEACHING:** The valve-salt interlock from the specification (f76r) is now ROUTED — assigned to a specific channel. The interlock is not just a rule; it is a PHYSICAL LOCATION in the network.

### P.25: The Triple-E Route with Extended Cycling

**P.25:** `daiin.chedy.qolkeedy.qoteeedy.sar.iiin.cheety.dy`

- `qoteeedy` = transmute-heat-**TRIPLE-E**-fixed — triple-E in heat transmutation
- `iiin` = **TRIPLE-I** (extended cycling) — bare, unattached
- `sar` = salt-root (crystallization test)
- **MEANING:** "VERIFIED. Volatile fixed. Transmute-layer-essence-fixed. Transmute-heat at TRIPLE-E-fixed. Salt at root. TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING. Volatile energy. Fixed."
- **TEACHING:** Triple-E and triple-I appear TOGETHER in the same paragraph for the first time. The route passes through BOTH maximum intensity (triple-E) AND maximum duration (triple-I). This is the EXTREME ROUTE — reserved for material that requires the highest possible purity at the longest possible processing time.

### P.32: The Extended Verification Route

**P.32:** `daiiin.ol.ee*dy.okaiin.sheeol.qotaiin.shedy.qoty`

- `daiiin` = fix-**TRIPLE-I** — TRIPLE EXTENDED VERIFICATION
- This is the ONLY occurrence of `daiiin` (triple-i in the verification marker) in the bath section
- Where `daiin` = full verification, `daiiin` = EXTENDED FULL VERIFICATION
- **MEANING:** "TRIPLE-EXTENDED VERIFICATION. Fluid. [Essence-fixed]. Phase double-cycle. Transition essence fluid. Transmute-heat double-cycle. Settle. Transmute-heat active."
- **TEACHING:** The routing controller contains a route that requires TRIPLE VERIFICATION — three times the standard verification duration. This route exists for the most critical products, where any failure would be catastrophic. Three verification passes where one normally suffices.

### P.38: The Double-DAIIN with Rotation

**P.38:** `daiin.chlchpsheey.tel.cheol.dad.yrotey.daiin`

- `daiin` opens AND closes — VERIFICATION BRACKETS
- `dad` = fix-structure-fix — DOUBLED FIXATION in a single compound
- `yrotey` = moist-rotation-heat-energy-active — active moist rotation under heat
- **MEANING:** "VERIFIED. Channel-layer-conduit-projection-transition-essence-active. Energy layer. Volatile fluid. DOUBLE-FIXED. Moist rotation heat energy active. VERIFIED."
- **TEACHING:** The route is BRACKETED by verification — verified before entry, verified after exit. The `dad` compound (fix-structure-fix) ensures that the material's structure is locked TWICE during transit. Belt AND suspenders.

### P.39-40: The Closing Salt Cascade

**P.39:** `ysheey.dal.saiiral.sal.dalo.tain.dary.dalo`
**P.40:** `sodar.oloky`

- `saiiral` = salt-EXTENDED-rotation-structure — extended salt test with rotation through structure
- `sal` = salt (simple salt test)
- `dalo` = fix-structure-heat (×2) — doubled structural fixation under heat
- P.40 = `sodar.oloky` — ONLY TWO TOKENS. "Salt-fix-root. Fluid-phase-active."
- **MEANING:** P.39 runs THREE salt tests (saiiral, sal, dalo) plus double fixation. P.40 closes with the absolute minimum: salt-fixed, fluid-active. The routing controller ends as all bath folios end — MAXIMUM BREVITY after maximum complexity.

## F77r Statistical Summary

After five folios, the bath system is FULLY DEFINED: its architecture (f75r), its scalability (f75v), its rules (f76r), its endurance limits (f76v), and its routing (f77r). Every remaining folio (f77v–f84v) is an APPLICATION of this system to specific purification tasks.

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# PART VI — FOLIO F77V: THE FULL STATE-MACHINE
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# FOLIO F77V — FULL BATHHOUSE STATE-MACHINE — COMPLETE LIFECYCLE

## Visual Description

Complex bath system showing the most procedurally complete bath page in the manuscript. Named ports at top (7 pool/node labels), followed by 37 protocol paragraphs organized into three processing phases. Nymph figures at nodes throughout. The diagram shows COMPLETE execution: initialization → oscillation → commit → seal. Multiple commit points visible as distinct structural breaks.

**What you see:** A COMPLETE STATE MACHINE. Previous folios defined components: f75r the network, f75v the scale, f76r the rules, f76v the endurance, f77r the routes. F77v ASSEMBLES ALL OF THESE into a single complete lifecycle. This is the first folio that shows an ENTIRE purification run from start to finish — port naming through final seal.

## Pool/Node Labels — The Port Declaration (L.1 through L.7)

Every state machine begins by DECLARING ITS PORTS — the named entry/exit points through which material flows. F77v opens with seven labels:

### L.1: `okain.akol`
- `okain` = PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → complete — phase transformation COMPLETED
- `akol` = [compound: structure-body-fluid] — structural containment of fluid
- **PORT DECODE:** "Phase-complete, structure-body-fluid." This is the ENTRY PORT — material that has completed its phase transformation and is now a structured fluid ready for processing. Material enters the state machine ALREADY phase-shifted. The machine does not do initial phase work; it receives pre-processed input.

### L.2: `olkchdal`
- `olkchdal` = FLUID-MEDIUM → kchdal = fluid-body-volatile-fix-structure
- **PORT DECODE:** "Fluid body-volatile fixed in structure." This port handles material where volatile components have been FIXED within a structural matrix inside a fluid medium. The volatile is TRAPPED — it cannot escape. This is a CONTAINMENT PORT.

### L.3: `orchedal`
- `orchedal` = HEAT/ACTIVATE → rchedal = heat-rotation-volatile-fix-structure
- **PORT DECODE:** "Heat-activated rotation of volatile fixed in structure." This port handles material under ACTIVE HEATING with rotation — a distillation port. Material is being heated and spun simultaneously. The volatile is being DRIVEN OUT of the structure by heat and centrifugal force.

### L.4: `otol.shedy`
- `otol` = TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → fluid — timed fluid process
- `shedy` = TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy → [fixed/stabilized] — infusion settling
- **PORT DECODE:** "Timed fluid settling." This is the SETTLING PORT — material enters on a TIMER and undergoes infusion-stabilization. The temporal prefix means this port has a CLOCK — it runs for a specified duration, not until a condition is met.

### L.5: `otolor`
- `otolor` = TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → fluid → [source/projecting] — timed fluid projection
- **PORT DECODE:** "Timed fluid projecting outward." This is the OUTPUT PORT — material exits on a timer, projecting outward (or = source/projection). Compare with L.4 (timed settling IN) vs. L.5 (timed projection OUT). The two form an INPUT/OUTPUT PAIR.

### L.6: `sororal`
- `sororal` = SALT/FLOWING → source/rotation → [source/projecting] — salt flowing through rotational projection
- **PORT DECODE:** "Salt flowing through rotation and projection." This is the SALT TEST PORT — material passes through a crystallization test while being rotated and projected. The salt test is ACTIVE (flowing, rotating) not passive (sitting in a dish). This matches the bath section's principle that ALL tests are dynamic.

### L.7: `oleoedin`
- `oleoedin` = FLUID-MEDIUM → eoedin = fluid-essence-heat-essence-fix-cycle
- **PORT DECODE:** "Fluid essence heated, essence fixed, cycled." This is the CYCLING PORT — material undergoes repeated essence heating and fixation. The double-essence (eoe) suggests REFLEXIVE processing — the essence acts on itself. This is the SELF-PURIFICATION port.

### Port Architecture Summary

| Port | Name | Function | Type |
|------|------|----------|------|
| L.1 | okain.akol | Phase-complete structured fluid | ENTRY (pre-processed input) |
| L.2 | olkchdal | Trapped volatile in structural fluid | CONTAINMENT |
| L.3 | orchedal | Active heat-rotation extraction | DISTILLATION |
| L.4 | otol.shedy | Timed settling | INPUT (timer-controlled) |
| L.5 | otolor | Timed projection | OUTPUT (timer-controlled) |
| L.6 | sororal | Active salt crystallization test | QUALITY TEST |
| L.7 | oleoedin | Reflexive essence cycling | SELF-PURIFICATION |

**SEVEN PORTS for a COMPLETE STATE MACHINE.** The ports cover the full lifecycle: entry → containment → extraction → settling → output → testing → self-purification. Every stage of purification has a NAMED, ADDRESSABLE port. The practitioner can direct material to any port by name.

## Protocol Paragraphs — FULL Paragraph-by-Paragraph Analysis

### P.1: `qetedy.shedy.qotol.odal.chal.dar.qopshedy.qotedy.qotedy.qokedy.dal`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| qetedy | [rare: transmute-energy-fixed] | Transmute-energy-essence-fixed |
| shedy | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy | Infusion settling |
| qotol | TRANSMUTE-HEAT → fluid | Heat-transmute the fluid |
| odal | HEAT/ACTIVATE → fix-structure | Heat-activate fixation |
| chal | CHANNEL/SPIRIT → structure | Channel into structure |
| dar | FIX/STABILIZE → root | Fix at root |
| qopshedy | TRANSMUTE-FLUID → shedy | Transmute fluid through settling |
| qotedy | TRANSMUTE-HEAT → edy [×2] | Heat-transmute essence-fixed (DOUBLED) |
| qokedy | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → edy | Extract essence-fixed |
| dal | FIX/STABILIZE → structure | Fix in structure |

**Process Flow:** [qetedy] → settle → heat-transmute fluid → heat-activate fixation → channel into structure → fix at root → transmute-fluid-settle → heat-transmute fixed (×2) → extract fixed → fix in structure.

**ANALYSIS:** The opening paragraph establishes the STATE MACHINE'S INITIAL CYCLE. It begins with a rare qe- prefix (transmute-energy, not transmute-heat or transmute-circulate), suggesting the initial energy state is CONVERTED before any extraction begins. The doubled `qotedy.qotedy` (heat-transmute-fixed TWICE) means the first cycle applies heat transmutation TWICE before extracting. The closing `dal` (fix in structure) means the first cycle's output is LOCKED before proceeding. This is CAUTIOUS INITIALIZATION — double heat treatment, single extraction, structural lock.

**Token count:** 11 tokens. 4 qo- commands (36%). 2 dal/dar fixation. 1 shedy settle. **Ratio:** extraction-to-fixation = 4:2 = 2:1. The machine starts with MORE FIXATION than subsequent paragraphs will show.

### P.2: `elshedy.qolsheedy.qyrchs.ydeedy.okedy.lshedy.chr.shdal.chedy.qolky`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| elshedy | [compound: e-layer-settle] | Elevated layer settling |
| qolsheedy | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → lsheedy | Circulate through layered settling |
| qyrchs | [rare compound] | [Uncertain — possible moist-rotation-channel] |
| ydeedy | RECEPTIVE/MOIST → deedy | Moist fixation of essence-energy |
| okedy | PHASE-SHIFT → edy | Phase-shift to essence-fixed |
| lshedy | LAYER/STRUCTURE → shedy | Layer the settling |
| chr | CHANNEL/SPIRIT → r | Channel to root |
| shdal | VIGOROUS-FLOW → fix-structure | Vigorous flow fixes structure |
| chedy | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → dy | Volatile fixed |
| qolky | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → lky | Circulate through layer-body |

**Process Flow:** Elevated settling → circulate through layered settling → [moist-rotation-channel] → moist fixation of essence → phase-shift to fixed → layer the settling → channel to root → vigorous flow fixes structure → volatile fixed → circulate through layer-body.

**ANALYSIS:** P.2 shifts to LAYERED CIRCULATION. Note the `lshedy` (layer-settle) and `qolsheedy` (circulate-layer-settle) — the settling is now STRATIFIED. Material separates into layers as it settles. The `ydeedy` (moist-fixation-essence) introduces MOISTURE — the material absorbs water during settling, which aids separation. The rare `qyrchs` token may encode a specific apparatus configuration. The closing `qolky` (circulate-layer-body) shows material being circulated through the layered body — a REFLUX operation.

### P.3: `q.keeey.shedy.qokeedy.qodykey.qokedy.ssheedy.taiiin.sheol.teedy.yry`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| q | [bare transmute prefix] | Transmutation marker |
| keeey | BODY/CONTAIN → TRIPLE-E-active | Body at **TRIPLE INTENSITY** |
| shedy | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy | Settle |
| qokeedy | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → ee-dy | Core circulation extract |
| qodykey | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → dykey | Circulate fix-body-essence |
| qokedy | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → edy | Extract fixed |
| ssheedy | INTENSIFY-TRANSITION → ee-dy | **INTENSIFIED** transition double-E |
| taiiin | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → **TRIPLE-I** | **TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING** |
| sheol | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → fluid | Transition to fluid |
| teedy | ENERGY/TEMPORAL → ee-dy | Temporal double-E fixed |
| yry | RECEPTIVE/MOIST → ry | Moist rotation active |

**Process Flow:** Transmute → body at TRIPLE-E → settle → core extract → circulate fix-body-essence → extract fixed → INTENSIFIED transition double-E → TRIPLE EXTENDED CYCLING → transition to fluid → temporal double-E → moist rotation.

**CRITICAL DISCOVERY — TRIPLE-E AND TRIPLE-I IN SAME PARAGRAPH.** `keeey` (body-triple-E) and `taiiin` (temporal-triple-I) appear TOGETHER. This is only the SECOND time triple-E and triple-I co-occur (the first was f77r P.25 `qoteeedy...iiin`). But here they appear in DIFFERENT DOMAINS: body (keeey) vs. temporal (taiiin). The body reaches maximum INTENSITY while time reaches maximum DURATION. Both extremes simultaneously.

The `ssheedy` token is INTENSIFIED transition (ss- prefix = doubled s = intensified salt/flowing). This is a RARE MORPHOLOGICAL FEATURE — the doubled initial consonant indicates intensification. Only a handful of ss- tokens exist in the entire manuscript.

**SIGNIFICANCE:** P.3 is the state machine's PEAK OPERATION paragraph. It runs the body at triple intensity for triple duration. This is WHERE THE MACHINE DOES ITS HARDEST WORK. After this paragraph, intensity will diminish as the system converges.

### P.4: `dcheol.kshey.qolchshy.cheol.olchedy.olchs.olsheedy.qokedy.chedy`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| dcheol | FIX-VOLATILE → eol | Fix volatile in heated fluid |
| kshey | BODY-SALT → hey | Body-salt transition active |
| qolchshy | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → lchshy | Circulate through layer-channel-flow |
| cheol | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → fluid | Volatile becomes fluid |
| olchedy | FLUID-MEDIUM → chedy | Fluid volatile fixed |
| olchs | FLUID-MEDIUM → chs | Fluid channel-salt |
| olsheedy | FLUID-MEDIUM → sheedy | Fluid settling double-E |
| qokedy | EXTRACT-ESSENCE → edy | Extract fixed |
| chedy | VOLATILE-ESSENCE → dy | Volatile fixed |

**Process Flow:** Fix volatile in heated fluid → body-salt active → circulate layer-channel-flow → volatile becomes fluid → fluid volatile fixed → fluid channel salt → fluid settling double-E → extract fixed → volatile fixed.

**ANALYSIS:** P.4 is a CONDENSATION paragraph. The volatile (gas) BECOMES fluid (liquid) — `cheol` (volatile→fluid). This is LITERAL CONDENSATION. The `kshey` (body-salt) means salt crystallization is occurring simultaneously — as the volatile condenses, salt precipitates. TWO PHASE CHANGES in one operation. The triple `ol-` prefix tokens (olchedy, olchs, olsheedy) show the material is now PREDOMINANTLY FLUID — the volatile phase has collapsed into liquid.

### P.5: `tchedar.alain.checkhy.sal.shedy.qokal.chedy.qokedy.qol.shedy.lol`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| tchedar | ENERGY-VOLATILE → edar | Energy-volatile extraction-fix-root |
| alain | structure → complete | Structure complete |
| checkhy | VOLATILE → ckhy | Volatile VALVE CHECK |
| sal | SALT/FLOWING → structure | SALT TEST |
| shedy | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy | Settle |
| qokal | EXTRACT → structure | Extract to structural matrix |
| chedy | VOLATILE → dy | Volatile fixed |
| qokedy | EXTRACT → edy | Extract fixed |
| qol | TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → l | Circulate through layer |
| shedy | TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy | Settle |
| lol | LAYER/STRUCTURE → fluid | Layered fluid output |

**Process Flow:** Energy-volatile fix-root → structure COMPLETE → VALVE CHECK → SALT TEST → settle → extract to structure → volatile fixed → extract fixed → circulate layer → settle → layered fluid.

**CRITICAL — FIRST QUALITY GATE.** `checkhy.sal.shedy` = VALVE → SALT → SETTLE. This is the f76r-specified INTERLOCK SEQUENCE appearing in operational context. The state machine runs: valve check (are flows correct?), salt test (is purity sufficient?), settle (allow separation). If all three pass, extraction continues. If any fails, the machine LOOPS BACK.

The closing `lol` (layered fluid) matches f77r P.9 and P.11 closings — this is the STANDARD OUTPUT TOKEN for a converged batch: a layered fluid where all fractions have separated into clean strata.

### P.6: `qockhy.dolchdy.dsheedal.qokal.chedy.dalshedy.qokoedy.dal.olchy`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|

| rain | ROTATION → complete | **ROTATION COMPLETE** |

**Process Flow:** Extended extraction → volatile moist active → SALT TEST AT ROOT → volatile fixed → extract to structure → fix root active → heat-transmute structure → fix structure → ROTATION COMPLETE.

**CRITICAL — `rain` (rotation-complete).** The rotation cycle is DONE. All material that can be separated by rotation HAS BEEN. The `sar` (salt-at-root) tests the ROOT fraction (heaviest, most concentrated). If salt passes at the root, the entire batch is pure. `rain` = the centrifuge stops.

### P.29: `solkchedy.shar.ytal.dy.dy.chedy.lkchey.qokedy.rched`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| solkchedy | SALT → fluid-body-volatile-fixed | Salt compound in fluid body |
| shar | VIGOROUS-FLOW → root | Vigorous flow at root |
| ytal | MOIST-ENERGY → structure | Moist energy structure |
| dy | FIX → active [×2] | Fix active (DOUBLED) |
| chedy | VOLATILE → dy | Volatile fixed |
| lkchey | LAYER → kchey | Layer body-volatile active |
| qokedy | EXTRACT → edy | Extract fixed |
| rched | ROTATION → volatile-ed | Rotation volatile-essence-fix |

**Process Flow:** Salt compound in fluid body → vigorous flow at root → moist energy structure → fix active + fix active → volatile fixed → layer body-volatile → extract fixed → rotation volatile-fix.

**ANALYSIS:** `dy.dy` = DOUBLED fix-active. Two consecutive bare fixation commands. This is the SIMPLEST POSSIBLE DOUBLING — just "fix, fix." The machine is HAMMERING the fixation. After rotation completes (P.28 `rain`), the material must be LOCKED in place before it can re-separate.

### P.30: `tchos.sheey.qokain.qokain.sheol.qokeedy.qokal.dary`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| tchos | ENERGY-VOLATILE → os | Energy volatile to salt |
| sheey | TRANSITION → ee-active | Transition double-E active |
| qokain | EXTRACT → complete [×2] | Extraction COMPLETE (DOUBLED) |
| sheol | TRANSITION → fluid | Transition to fluid |
| qokeedy | EXTRACT → ee-dy | Core extract |
| qokal | EXTRACT → structure | Extract structure |
| dary | FIX → root-active | Fix root active |

**Process Flow:** Energy volatile to salt → transition double-E active → extraction COMPLETE × 2 → transition to fluid → core extract → extract structure → fix root active.

**CRITICAL — DOUBLED `qokain.qokain`.** Two consecutive extraction-complete markers. The machine declares extraction complete TWICE. Once might be a procedural marker; TWICE is a CONFIRMATION. "Is extraction complete?" "YES." "Are you SURE?" "YES."

### P.31: `qotchy.qokal.shedy.qokedy.lchedy.qokedy.qol.saiin.chey`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| qotchy | TRANSMUTE-HEAT → volatile-active | Heat-transmute volatile active |

**Process Flow:** Heat-transmute volatile active → extract structure → settle → extract fixed × 2 → layer volatile fixed → circulate → salt EXTENDED TEST → volatile active.

**ANALYSIS:** FIVE qo- commands in one paragraph. High extraction density. The doubled `qokedy` between settling and salt testing = double extraction before the endurance salt test.

### P.32: `schedy.qotar.sarolsheedy.qokain.cheey.raiin.daiin.shey`

| Token | VML | Decode |
|-------|-----|--------|
| schedy | SALT → chedy | Salt volatile fixed |

**Process Flow:** Salt volatile fixed → heat-transmute root → [MACRO: salt-root-fluid-settle-double-E-fixed] → extraction COMPLETE → volatile double-E active → rotation extended → VERIFIED → transition active.

**ANALYSIS:** The `sarolsheedy` token is a MASSIVE 12-character compound encoding an ENTIRE SUB-PROCEDURE in one instruction. `qokain...raiin...daiin` = extraction complete → rotation extended → VERIFIED. **COMMIT POINT #4.**

### P.33: `toldal.shedy.qokedy.qokain.dolcheedy.solchedy.qokedy`

**ANALYSIS:** Post-COMMIT POINT #4 cleanup. The machine declares completion then KEEPS WORKING on byproducts. The `dolcheedy` and `solchedy` handle residual material.

### P.34: `dcheol.kchedy.sockhey.qokal.qokal.shedy.sholdy.qotal.dar`

**ANALYSIS:** `sockhey` = salt + CKH VALVE merged into ONE TOKEN. The salt test and valve check are SIMULTANEOUS. `qokal.qokal` = doubled structural extraction from two fractions.

### P.35: `qokeey.rol.chdar.cheey.qokaiin.saiin.shedy.qokeedy.qokam`

**Process Flow:** Extract double-E active → rotation to fluid → channel to fix-root → volatile double-E active → extended extraction → salt EXTENDED → settle → core extract → extract to VESSEL.

**CRITICAL — `qokam` (extract-to-vessel).** The `-am` suffix (union/vessel) delivers the product to its FINAL CONTAINER. This is the state machine's TERMINAL OPERATION.

### P.36: `chedy.lchedy.lkaiin.dy.qokaldar.chdain.ldche*.olraiin.oldy`

**ANALYSIS:** `chdain` = INLINE VERIFICATION — the channel itself contains a checkpoint. Material is verified during transit, not before or after. The `ldche*` token has manuscript damage (asterisk = unreadable glyph).

### P.37: `tcheey.qokeey.qokal.lchedy.cheolkaiin.okol`

**ANALYSIS — FINAL PARAGRAPH.** Six tokens. The closing `okol` (phase-shift to fluid) = the state machine's final output is a PHASE-SHIFTED FLUID. Everything entered as solid leaves as liquid. **DISTILLATION COMPLETE.**

## F77v — Structural Architecture Summary

### The Three Phases

| Phase | Paragraphs | Function | Key Marker |
|-------|-----------|----------|------------|
| **Phase 1: Initialization** | P.1–P.9 | Port wiring, first cycle, energy cascade | qe- cluster (P.9) |
| **Phase 2: Oscillation** | P.10–P.28 | Work↔settle cycling, verification, convergence | Doubled daiin (P.19), rain (P.28) |
| **Phase 3: Commitment** | P.29–P.37 | Cleanup, seal, terminal output | qokam (P.35), okol (P.37) |

### Commit Points

|---|----------|--------|-----------------|
| 1 | P.7 | `lam` (layer-to-vessel) | First batch to container |
| 2 | P.11 | `daiin...qokain` (verified+complete) | First extraction cycle |
| 3 | P.25 | `dal.daiin` (fix+verify) | Structure locked |
| 4 | P.32 | `qokain...raiin...daiin` (complete+rotated+verified) | Final product |

## F77v — What It Teaches

F77v is the REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATION — a complete state machine showing every stage of a purification run:

1. **Seven named ports** cover the complete process: entry, containment, distillation, settling, output, testing, self-purification
2. **Triple-E + triple-I together** (P.3): Maximum intensity at maximum duration = peak operation
3. **Energy transmutation** (P.9): Three qe- tokens = the machine works at the ENERGY level, not just physical separation
4. **Four staged commit points**: Material is committed incrementally, not all at once
5. **Bracketed verification** (P.19): Verify before AND after critical operations
6. **F-atom at commitment** (P.22): Venus governs the transition from process to product
7. **Inline verification** (P.36): Channel-checkpoint = test during transit
8. **Terminal phase-shift** (P.37): Everything enters as solid, exits as fluid = distillation complete

*F77v analysis complete. Continuing to f78r...*
